# All covered MEP vote records — 2021 to 2026

This table joins every person appearing in the seven included material plenary roll calls: **1170 people**. Historical ballot membership, country and EP group come from the roll-call source; public contact enrichment is only supplied for people in the live 2026 EP roster.

Every unresolved non-vote in the seven tracked ballots is matched against the official attendance register for the same sitting. `no vote — present` means recorded present for the sitting; `no vote — not recorded present` does not establish physical absence at the ballot or its reason.
